The infamous cake shot

While attempting to make this otherwise undistinguished photo, I unfortunately let the tripod with the camera on it tip and bash my camera, causing some cosmetic damage to the body but more significantly breaking its autoexposure function.  So, I had to shoot the party on manual exposure and a lot of my guesses were pretty far from what they should have been... Camera has gone to the shop and I hope they can fix it.

Explore your options for ridesharing

Hundreds of these little classical kites were strung at seven foot intervals on a line.  The owner kept pulling more and more out of a cardboard box, like a magician pulling ribbons out of his mouth.  Despite so many kites supplying lift, they weren't very strong, easily manageable by a single person.

##-----------------TITLE------------------------##
Kelvin Foam
##------------------TEXT------------------------##
Prev: Platonic SkeletonsUp: David Gunderson's mathematical modelsNext: Truncated Dodecahedron
Kelvin Foam

Another tessellation of space by zonohedra (truncated octahedra).
Kelvin conjectured incorrectly that this tesselation, more formally known as the
bitruncated cubic honeycomb,
is the most efficient way to partition space into unit-volume cells (as measured by the surface area of the cells).
However, a different tessellation, the Weaire–Phelan structure, has even smaller surface area.
